FFinRED: An Expert-Guided Benchmark Generation and Evaluation Framework for Financial LLM Red-Teaming
Authors: Chaeyun Kim, Daeyoung Park, Junghwan Kim, Jinyoung Jeong, Eunji Song, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
First: 2026-06-18T07:46:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-18T07:46:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing safety benchmarks target general adversarial scenarios but miss finance-specific risks. Financial LLMs face regulatory compliance violations, fraud facilitation, and systemic trust erosion that require targeted evaluation. We introduce FinRED, an expert-guided red-teaming framework for financial LLM safety evaluation developed with financial experts. FinRED uses a novel two-level taxonomy mapping global standards (e.g., FATF and EU DORA) to threats ranging from regulatory evasion to complex fraud, integrated with a scalable pipeline that converts real financial documents into context-rich red-teaming Behavioral Prompts (seeds) through an expert-defined schema. Rigorous expert validation confirms seed plausibility and realism for meaningful LLM safety evaluation. We also provide an expert-validated, finance-specific rubric that goes beyond disclaimer checks, aligns more closely with human experts than static one-size-fits-all rubrics, and reduces critical false negatives from 28 to 12. Aligned with internationally adopted risk-management and information-security standards (e.g., ISO/IEC 27001), FinRED is deployed in South Korea's Financial Security Institute (FSI) regulatory sandbox for generative AI security evaluation in real financial services. To mitigate dual-use risks, the dataset, generation pipeline, prompt template, and evaluation framework are gated for qualified researchers at https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper and https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FFinRED：一个专家指导的金融LLM红队基准生成与评估框架
现有的安全基准针对一般对抗场景，但忽视了金融特定风险。金融LLM面临合规性违规、欺诈促进和系统性信任侵蚀等问题，需要针对性评估。我们引入了FinRED，这是一个由金融专家开发的专家指导的金融LLM安全评估红队框架。FinRED使用一种新颖的两级分类法，将全球标准（如FATF和EU DORA）映射到从合规规避到复杂欺诈的威胁，结合一个可扩展的管道，通过专家定义的模式将真实金融文档转换为上下文丰富的红队行为提示（种子）。严格的专家验证确认了种子的合理性和真实性，以便进行有意义的LLM安全评估。我们还提供了一个经过专家验证的金融特定评分标准，超越了免责声明检查，更加贴近人类专家，而不是静态的一刀切评分标准，并将关键的假阴性从28减少到12。与国际公认的风险管理和信息安全标准（如ISO/IEC 27001）一致，FinRED在韩国金融安全研究所（FSI）的监管沙箱中部署，用于真实金融服务中的生成AI安全评估。为了减轻双重用途风险，数据集、生成管道、提示模板和评估框架对合格研究人员进行了限制，网址为https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper和https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the inadequacy of existing safety benchmarks for financial LLMs, which often overlook finance-specific risks such as regulatory compliance violations and fraud. Previous methods have primarily focused on general adversarial scenarios, leading to a lack of targeted evaluation for financial contexts. The proposed FinRED framework distinguishes itself by integrating expert guidance to create a two-level taxonomy that maps global standards to specific threats, while also employing a scalable pipeline to generate context-rich red-teaming prompts from real financial documents. This approach is well-motivated as it aligns with international risk-management standards and has been validated by experts to ensure seed plausibility. The contribution of this paper lies in its expert-validated rubric that significantly reduces false negatives in safety evaluations, achieving a reduction from 28 to 12. FinRED has been deployed in South Korea's Financial Security Institute regulatory sandbox, demonstrating its effectiveness in evaluating generative AI security in real financial services.
本研究解决了现有金融大型语言模型（LLM）安全基准不足的问题，这些基准主要关注一般对抗场景，忽视了诸如合规违规和欺诈等金融特定风险。以往的方法缺乏针对性的评估框架，导致在评估LLM安全性时出现关键的假阴性。所提出的FinRED框架与金融专家共同开发，引入了一个两级分类法，将全球标准映射到特定威胁，并利用可扩展的管道从真实金融文档中创建上下文丰富的红队提示。这种方法的动机充分，因为它与国际风险管理标准相一致，并经过专家验证，以增强安全评估的可信性和现实性。本文的贡献在于其专家指导的评分标准显著减少了假阴性，并在生成AI安全评估的监管沙箱中部署，实现了在识别金融服务特定风险方面的性能提升。
SPHINX: First Explain, Then Explore
Authors: Nguyen Do, Tue M. Cao, Tien Van Do, András Hajdu, Tamás Bérczes, My T. Thai
First: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00
Comments: 13 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generating adversarial driving scenarios is critical for evaluating and improving autonomous vehicle decision-making systems in simulation. Recent approaches, such as ChatScene and LLM-Attacker, rely primarily on the prior knowledge of Large Language Models and Vision-Language Models to generate driving scenarios procedurally. We argue that adversarial scenes should be generated based on the failure diagnosis (e.g., indecisiveness, multi-frame inconsistency) of the driving policy to specifically address the policy's weaknesses instead of relying on prior assumptions. In this paper, we propose SPHINX, a closed-loop framework for adversarial scenario synthesis guided by a simple principle: first explain, then explore. Beyond blindly exploring the scenario space, SPHINX leverages explainable artificial intelligence methods to analyze the policy, identifying key visual concepts and their influence on policy outputs, and the uncertainty of the decisions. Given the interpretable evidence extracted from the policy's own decision process, we use a vision language model to rationalize and criticize failure modes of the current policy. These critics are then used to generate targeted adversarial scenarios for policy retraining and improvement. We demonstrate that SPHINX can highlight an interpretable account of policy failures while other adversarial scene generation cannot. Across the evaluated benchmarks and test suites, SPHINX can be applied to diverse state-of-the-art autonomous vehicle architectures and yields consistent robustness improvements over existing scenario-generation methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPHINX：先解释，再探索
生成对抗驾驶场景对于评估和改进自主车辆决策系统在仿真中的表现至关重要。最近的方法，如ChatScene和LLM-Attacker，主要依赖于大型语言模型和视觉-语言模型的先验知识来程序化生成驾驶场景。我们认为，对抗场景应基于驾驶策略的失败诊断（例如，优柔寡断、多帧不一致）生成，以具体解决策略的弱点，而不是依赖先前假设。本文提出了SPHINX，一个闭环框架，用于对抗场景合成，其指导原则是：先解释，再探索。SPHINX不仅仅是盲目探索场景空间，而是利用可解释人工智能方法分析策略，识别关键视觉概念及其对策略输出的影响，以及决策的不确定性。根据从策略自身决策过程中提取的可解释证据，我们使用视觉语言模型来合理化和批评当前策略的失败模式。这些批评随后用于生成针对性的对抗场景，以进行策略再训练和改进。我们证明SPHINX能够突出政策失败的可解释性，而其他对抗场景生成方法则无法做到。在评估的基准和测试套件中，SPHINX可以应用于多种最先进的自主车辆架构，并在现有场景生成方法上实现一致的鲁棒性提升。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the need for generating adversarial driving scenarios to enhance the evaluation and improvement of autonomous vehicle decision-making systems. Previous methods, such as ChatScene and LLM-Attacker, primarily depend on the prior knowledge of Large Language Models and Vision-Language Models, which may not effectively target specific weaknesses in driving policies. The proposed SPHINX framework differs by focusing on failure diagnosis of the driving policy, utilizing explainable artificial intelligence to analyze and identify key visual concepts influencing policy outputs. This approach allows for the generation of targeted adversarial scenarios that are directly informed by the policy's failures, leading to improved retraining and robustness. The methodology demonstrates that SPHINX can provide interpretable insights into policy failures and achieves consistent performance improvements across various benchmarks compared to existing methods.
本研究旨在有效生成对抗性驾驶场景，以增强对自动驾驶决策系统的评估。以往的方法，如ChatScene和LLM-Attacker，主要依赖大型语言模型和视觉-语言模型的先验知识，可能忽视驾驶策略中的具体弱点。所提出的SPHINX框架通过关注驾驶策略的失败诊断而有所不同，利用可解释的人工智能分析决策过程，识别影响政策输出的关键视觉概念。这种方法使得能够生成针对特定弱点的对抗性场景，从而有助于改进策略再训练。SPHINX被证明能够提供对政策失败的可解释见解，并在各种基准和测试套件中相比现有方法实现了一致的鲁棒性提升。
Enhancing LLM Safety Through a Theoretical Minimax Game Lens
Authors: Yihe Deng, Yu Yang, Junkai Zhang, Wei Wang, Bo Li
First: 2025-02-07T18:45:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-15T02:50:15+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 9 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) necessitates effective mechanisms to ensure their responsible deployment by accurately distinguishing unsafe content from benign content. While substantial safety datasets are available in English, multilingual safety modeling remains underexplored due to limited open-source safety datasets in other languages. Even within English datasets, safe yet sensitive corner-case content is scarce, leading to shortcut learning by models and non-trivial false-positive rates. To mitigate these issues, we introduce a novel minimax reinforcement learning (RL) framework wherein a data generator and a classifier model co-evolve, facilitating the production of high-quality synthetic multilingual safety data. We theoretically formalize this interaction as a minimax game and rigorously demonstrate convergence to a Nash equilibrium. Empirical evaluations confirm that our synthetic data generation method significantly enhances the classifier model performance, enabling a substantially smaller model to surpass the state-of-the-art by nearly 10% on English benchmarks while achieving 4.5x faster inference speed. These results establish a scalable and efficient methodology for synthetic data generation, advancing the development of safer and more robust multilingual LLM deployments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过理论最小最大博弈视角增强大型语言模型安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展需要有效机制，以确保其负责任的部署，准确区分不安全内容与良性内容。虽然英语中有大量安全数据集，但由于其他语言中开放源代码安全数据集有限，多语言安全建模仍未得到充分探索。即使在英语数据集中，安全但敏感的边缘案例内容也很稀缺，导致模型的捷径学习和非平凡的误报率。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了一种新颖的最小最大强化学习（RL）框架，其中数据生成器和分类模型共同进化，促进高质量合成多语言安全数据的生成。我们将这种交互理论化为最小最大博弈，并严格证明其收敛到纳什均衡。实证评估确认，我们的合成数据生成方法显著提升了分类模型的性能，使得一个显著更小的模型在英语基准测试中超越了最先进的技术近10%，同时实现了4.5倍的推理速度提升。这些结果建立了一种可扩展且高效的合成数据生成方法，推动了更安全、更强大的多语言LLM部署的发展。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the urgent need for effective safety mechanisms in large language models (LLMs) due to their rapid advancement and the challenges in distinguishing unsafe from benign content, particularly in multilingual contexts. Previous methods have relied on limited English safety datasets and have struggled with issues such as shortcut learning and high false-positive rates. The proposed approach introduces a minimax reinforcement learning framework that allows a data generator and classifier to co-evolve, producing high-quality synthetic multilingual safety data and formalizing this interaction as a minimax game. This methodology is well-motivated as it addresses the scarcity of diverse safety data and enhances model robustness. Empirical results demonstrate that the proposed method improves classifier performance significantly, enabling a smaller model to outperform state-of-the-art benchmarks by nearly 10% in English while achieving a 4.5x faster inference speed, thus supporting the goal of safer multilingual LLM deployments.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）在区分不安全内容与良性内容方面的有效安全机制的迫切需求，特别是在多语言安全数据集有限的背景下。以往的方法在安全但敏感的边缘案例内容稀缺的情况下，导致模型出现捷径学习和高误报率。所提出的方法引入了一种极小极大强化学习框架，使数据生成器和分类器能够共同演化，生成高质量的多语言安全合成数据，并将这种交互理论化为极小极大博弈。该方法显著提高了分类器的性能，实证结果显示在英语基准测试中比最先进的模型提高了近10%，推理速度提高了4.5倍，从而为更安全、更强大的多语言LLM应用做出了贡献。
GAS-Leak-LLM: Genetic Algorithm-Based Suffix Optimization for Black-Box LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Aman Anifer, Vignesh Kumar Kembu, Vishnu M, Antonino Nocera, Vinod P., Amal Murali PK, Akshay S Rajan
First: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) constitute pivotal components within the AI-dominated information technology ecosystem. To mitigate risks associated with harmful or policy-violating outputs, commercial systems employ advanced alignment strategies and multi-layered content moderation mechanisms. Despite these safeguards, recent research has demonstrated that LLMs remain vulnerable to adversarial manipulation, particularly through jailbreaking and prompt injection techniques. In this work, we propose GAS-Leak-LLM a novel jailbreaking attack based on a genetic algorithm that systematically evolves adversarial suffix to bypass safety constraints. Operating in a strict black-box setting, our method requires no access to model parameters or internals, thereby reflecting realistic threat scenarios in deployed systems. Through the iterative application of selection, mutation, and crossover heuristics, the framework systematically explores the discrete prompt space to identify high-fitness adversarial suffixes. Empirical findings reveal critical shortcomings in existing safety enforcement mechanisms and confirm the effectiveness and practical viability of the proposed attack.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GAS-Leak-LLM：基于遗传算法的黑箱LLM越狱后缀优化
大型语言模型（LLMs）是AI主导的信息技术生态系统中的关键组成部分。为了减轻与有害或违反政策输出相关的风险，商业系统采用先进的对齐策略和多层次内容审核机制。尽管有这些保护措施，最近的研究表明，LLMs仍然容易受到对抗性操控，特别是通过越狱和提示注入技术。在本研究中，我们提出了GAS-Leak-LLM，一种基于遗传算法的新型越狱攻击，系统地演化对抗性后缀以绕过安全约束。在严格的黑箱环境中，我们的方法不需要访问模型参数或内部结构，从而反映了已部署系统中的现实威胁场景。通过选择、变异和交叉启发式的迭代应用，该框架系统地探索离散提示空间，以识别高适应性的对抗性后缀。实证研究揭示了现有安全执行机制的关键缺陷，并确认了所提攻击的有效性和实际可行性。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the vulnerabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) to adversarial manipulation, particularly through jailbreaking and prompt injection techniques, despite existing alignment strategies and content moderation mechanisms. Previous methods have struggled to effectively prevent such attacks, highlighting the need for a more robust approach. The proposed method, GAS-Leak-LLM, utilizes a genetic algorithm to evolve adversarial suffixes in a black-box setting, which does not require access to model internals, thus simulating real-world threat scenarios. This approach is well-motivated as it systematically explores the prompt space using selection, mutation, and crossover heuristics to identify effective adversarial suffixes. The research demonstrates significant shortcomings in current safety mechanisms and shows that GAS-Leak-LLM can successfully bypass these constraints, confirming its effectiveness in practical applications.

CHILLGuard: Towards Fine-Grained Chinese LLM Safety Guardrail with Scalable Data Construction and Model-aware Preference Alignment
Authors: Wenbo Yu, Bohua Wang, Hao Fang, Kuofeng Gao, Jingru Zeng, Xiaochen Yang, Tianyi Zhang, Xiaoxiao Ma, Jiawei Kong, Hao Wu, Bin Chen, Shu-Tao Xia, Min Zhang
First: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Malicious content generated from large language models (LLMs) could pose severe safety risks and ethical concerns. While existing LLM safety guardrails excel in English or multilingual settings, they lack adaptation to Chinese-specific regulatory policies, cultural context and linguistic nuances, failing to support fine-grained risk classification for diverse deployment needs. In this paper, we introduce a 5-macro, 31-micro category fine-grained risk taxonomy for Chinese scenarios, and build CHILLGuard: a dedicated Chinese LLM content safety guardrail. To address the critical scarcity of high-quality annotated Chinese safety data, we propose a scalable multi-stage data construction pipeline: we expand multi-source corpus via retrieval-augmented generation, generate implicit harmful samples through prompt engineering rewriting, and refine high-quality data via multi-model voting-based label calibration. Based on this, we build CHILLGuardTrain, a large-scale training set with 405,007 samples, and CHILLGuardTest, a rigorously curated annotated test set with 51,745 samples. We then train CHILLGuard on CHILLGuardTrain under a generator-classifier collaborative framework via Model-aware Direct Preference Optimization. Extensive experiments under multiple settings demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of CHILLGuard, e.g., a 15.92% improvement of F1 score over Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict on our benchmark. We will release our resources at https://github.com/cswbyu/CHILLGuard.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHILLGuard：面向细粒度中文LLM安全防护的可扩展数据构建与模型感知偏好对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）生成的恶意内容可能带来严重的安全风险和伦理问题。现有的LLM安全防护在英语或多语言环境中表现出色，但缺乏对中国特定监管政策、文化背景和语言细微差别的适应，无法支持多样化部署需求的细粒度风险分类。本文提出了一种针对中文场景的5个宏观、31个微观类别的细粒度风险分类法，并构建了CHILLGuard：一个专门的中文LLM内容安全防护。为了解决高质量标注中文安全数据的严重短缺，我们提出了一种可扩展的多阶段数据构建流程：通过检索增强生成扩展多源语料，通过提示工程重写生成隐性有害样本，并通过多模型投票的标签校准精炼高质量数据。在此基础上，我们构建了CHILLGuardTrain，一个包含405,007个样本的大规模训练集，以及CHILLGuardTest，一个经过严格策划的标注测试集，包含51,745个样本。然后，我们在CHILLGuardTrain上通过模型感知直接偏好优化的生成器-分类器协作框架训练CHILLGuard。在多种设置下的广泛实验表明，CHILLGuard的性能达到了最先进水平，例如，在我们的基准测试中，F1分数比Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict提高了15.92%。我们将把我们的资源发布在https://github.com/cswbyu/CHILLGuard。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the safety risks and ethical concerns associated with malicious content generated by large language models (LLMs), particularly in the context of Chinese language and culture, where existing safety guardrails are inadequate. Previous methods have primarily focused on English or multilingual applications, lacking the necessary adaptation to Chinese-specific regulatory policies and linguistic nuances, which has resulted in ineffective risk classification. The proposed approach, CHILLGuard, introduces a fine-grained risk taxonomy tailored for Chinese scenarios and employs a scalable multi-stage data construction pipeline to generate high-quality annotated safety data. The methodology includes retrieval-augmented generation, prompt engineering for harmful sample generation, and multi-model voting for label calibration, resulting in a comprehensive training set of 405,007 samples and a test set of 51,745 samples. Experimental results demonstrate that CHILLGuard achieves state-of-the-art performance, with a 15.92% improvement in F1 score over existing models, effectively supporting the goal of enhancing safety in Chinese LLM applications.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）生成的恶意内容所带来的安全风险和伦理问题，特别是现有安全防护措施在中国特定监管和文化背景下的不足。以往的方法在细粒度风险分类方面存在困难，并且缺乏高质量的中文标注数据。所提出的方法CHILLGuard引入了全面的细粒度风险分类法和可扩展的数据构建流程，通过多源语料库扩展和模型投票进行标签校准，提高数据质量。该方法论生成了大规模训练集和严格策划的测试集，使得CHILLGuard能够在协作框架下进行训练，优化模型偏好。实验结果显示显著提升，F1分数比现有模型提高了15.92%，从而支持了在中文LLM应用中有效内容安全的目标。
Do You Really Need a GPU to Guard Your LLM? CPU-Class Classifiers and Multi-Stage Pipelines for Safety Enforcement at Scale
Authors: Vasudev Majhi, Dhruv Gupta, Advait Singh, Matthew Barker, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2025-12-22T04:00:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T05:46:54+00:00
Comments: Under Review. 25 pages, 5 figures, 38 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety classifiers that screen LLM inputs for jailbreak attempts have become standard deployment components, yet almost all production systems rely on GPU-based models: fine-tuned transformers and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines. These approaches impose significant per-query latency and infrastructure cost. Very little research has asked whether CPU-based classifiers, such as support vector machines and gradient-boosted trees trained on TF-IDF features, can match their accuracy across the conditions that production deployments encounter. We evaluate five CPU classifier families, Mamba-130M as an SSM-based GPU classifier, and transformer-based GPU models (DeBERTa-v3 and Gemma-2B with LoRA) across nine jailbreak sources and three regimes: in-distribution (D1), out-of-distribution (D2), and adversarially obfuscated (D3). On D1, the best CPU classifier matches the best transformer GPU model at roughly one-fifth the deployment cost. On D2, CPU classifiers fail via confident miscalibration, producing high-confidence false negatives that bypass escalation entirely. On D3, CPU classifiers outperform transformer GPU models by more than 26 percentage points in F1. Based on these complementary failure modes, we design GuardChain, a three-stage safety pipeline (Regex -> CPU -> GPU) that routes each prompt to the cheapest stage capable of a confident decision. The CPU stage alone resolves 80\% of in-distribution prompts at near-peak accuracy, and the GPU stage recovers the out-of-distribution failures. For practitioners deploying LLM safety at scale, this work provides evidence that GPU-class infrastructure is unnecessary for the majority of traffic.
中文标题/摘要
标题：您真的需要 GPU 来保护您的 LLM 吗？用于安全执行的 CPU 类分类器和多阶段管道
用于筛查 LLM 输入以防止越狱尝试的安全分类器已成为标准部署组件，但几乎所有生产系统都依赖于基于 GPU 的模型：微调的变换器和 LLM 作为裁判的管道。这些方法在每个查询上都带来了显著的延迟和基础设施成本。很少有研究探讨基于 CPU 的分类器，如支持向量机和基于 TF-IDF 特征训练的梯度提升树，是否能在生产部署所遇到的条件下匹配其准确性。 我们评估了五个 CPU 分类器系列，Mamba-130M 作为基于 SSM 的 GPU 分类器，以及基于变换器的 GPU 模型（DeBERTa-v3 和 Gemma-2B 与 LoRA）在九个越狱来源和三个模式下的表现：分布内（D1）、分布外（D2）和对抗性混淆（D3）。在 D1 中，最佳 CPU 分类器的表现与最佳变换器 GPU 模型相当，部署成本约为其五分之一。在 D2 中，CPU 分类器因自信的错误校准而失败，产生高置信度的假阴性，完全绕过升级。在 D3 中，CPU 分类器在 F1 上的表现超过变换器 GPU 模型超过 26 个百分点。 基于这些互补的失败模式，我们设计了 GuardChain，一个三阶段安全管道（Regex -> CPU -> GPU），将每个提示路由到能够做出自信决策的最便宜阶段。仅 CPU 阶段就以接近峰值的准确率解决了 80% 的分布内提示，而 GPU 阶段则恢复了分布外的失败。对于大规模部署 LLM 安全的从业者而言，这项工作提供了证据，表明 GPU 类基础设施对于大多数流量来说并非必要。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the growing need for safety classifiers in large language models (LLMs) to prevent jailbreak attempts, which traditionally rely on GPU-based models that incur high latency and costs. Previous methods predominantly utilized fine-tuned transformers and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines, leading to significant infrastructure expenses and performance issues, particularly in handling out-of-distribution inputs. The proposed approach introduces CPU-based classifiers, such as support vector machines and gradient-boosted trees, which demonstrate comparable accuracy to GPU models while significantly reducing costs. The study evaluates these classifiers across various scenarios and develops GuardChain, a three-stage safety pipeline that efficiently routes prompts based on their characteristics. The findings reveal that the CPU stage can accurately handle 80% of in-distribution prompts, while the GPU stage effectively addresses out-of-distribution failures, indicating that GPU infrastructure may not be necessary for most LLM safety deployments.
本研究关注于大型语言模型（LLM）中用于筛查输入以防止越狱尝试的安全分类器对GPU模型的依赖，这导致了高延迟和基础设施成本。以往的方法主要使用微调的变换器和LLM作为判断管道，但这些方法在成本和效率上存在显著缺陷。提出的方法引入了基于CPU的分类器，如支持向量机和梯度提升树，这些分类器在实现与GPU模型相当的准确性同时，显著降低了部署成本。研究评估了不同条件下的各种CPU分类器与GPU模型的表现，发现最佳的CPU分类器在成本的五分之一下与最佳的变换器GPU模型的性能相匹配，并在对抗场景中表现更佳。本文贡献了一个新颖的三阶段安全管道GuardChain，能够有效地将提示路由到最具成本效益的分类器，证明在大规模LLM安全执行中，GPU基础设施通常是不必要的。
NeST: Neuron Selective Tuning for LLM Safety
Authors: Sasha Behrouzi, Lichao Wu, Mohamadreza Rostami, Ahmad-Reza Sadeghi
First: 2026-02-18T20:01:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-12T11:06:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment is essential for the responsible deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs). Yet, existing approaches often rely on heavyweight fine-tuning that is costly to update, audit, and maintain across model families. Full fine-tuning incurs substantial computational and storage overhead, while parameter-efficient methods, e.g., Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), trade efficiency for inconsistent safety gains and sensitivity to design choices. Safety intervention mechanisms reduce unsafe outputs without modifying model weights, but do not directly shape or preserve the internal representations that govern safety behavior. We present NeST, a Neuron-Selective Tuning framework for efficient post-hoc safety alignment. NeST identifies safety-relevant feed-forward neurons via activation probing on vanilla harmful and benign prompts, clusters neurons with similar activation profiles, and trains shared cluster-level updates while freezing the rest of the model. Importantly, NeST is trained only on vanilla malicious prompts, without using jailbreak-specific attack data, yet generalizes robustly to diverse jailbreaks. The learned updates are then folded into the original weights, incurring no inference-time overhead. Evaluated on 14 open-weight language and multimodal models, NeST outperforms lightweight baselines and approaches full fine-tuning robustness with significantly fewer trainable parameters. On text-only models, NeST reduces average jailbreak attack success rate from 44.5% to 1.1% while training only 0.4M parameters on average. Across multimodal settings, it reduces ASR from 55.3% to 1.1%, and for downstream fine-tuned variants, it restores safety by reducing ASR from 53.8% to 0.8%. These results show that robust, maintainable safety alignment can be achieved by concentrating adaptation on localized, functionally coherent safety structures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：NeST：用于大型语言模型安全的神经元选择性调优
安全对齐对于大型语言模型（LLMs）的负责任部署至关重要。然而，现有方法通常依赖于成本高昂的重调优，难以在模型家族中进行更新、审计和维护。完全调优会产生大量的计算和存储开销，而参数高效的方法，如低秩适应（LoRA），则在效率与安全收益不一致和对设计选择敏感之间进行权衡。安全干预机制在不修改模型权重的情况下减少不安全输出，但并未直接塑造或保留影响安全行为的内部表示。 我们提出了NeST，一种用于高效事后安全对齐的神经元选择性调优框架。NeST通过对普通有害和良性提示的激活探测，识别与安全相关的前馈神经元，聚类具有相似激活特征的神经元，并在冻结模型其余部分的同时训练共享的聚类级更新。重要的是，NeST仅在普通恶意提示上进行训练，而不使用特定于越狱的攻击数据，但能够稳健地推广到多种越狱场景。学习到的更新随后被折叠到原始权重中，不会增加推理时的开销。在14个开放权重的语言和多模态模型上进行评估，NeST的表现优于轻量级基线，并以显著更少的可训练参数接近完全调优的鲁棒性。在仅文本模型上，NeST将平均越狱攻击成功率从44.5%降低到1.1%，同时平均仅训练0.4M参数。在多模态设置中，它将ASR从55.3%降低到1.1%，对于下游微调变体，它通过将ASR从53.8%降低到0.8%来恢复安全。这些结果表明，通过集中适应于局部、功能一致的安全结构，可以实现稳健、可维护的安全对齐。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for safety alignment in the deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs), highlighting the limitations of existing methods such as full fine-tuning, which is resource-intensive, and parameter-efficient approaches like Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), which compromise safety consistency. The proposed Neuron-Selective Tuning (NeST) framework offers a novel solution by selectively tuning only the safety-relevant neurons identified through activation probing, allowing for efficient post-hoc safety alignment without altering the entire model. This method is well-motivated as it reduces computational overhead while maintaining robust safety performance. NeST has been evaluated on 14 language and multimodal models, achieving significant reductions in jailbreak attack success rates, from 44.5% to 1.1% for text-only models and from 55.3% to 1.1% for multimodal settings, demonstrating that effective safety alignment can be achieved with minimal parameter adjustments.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）部署中安全对齐的关键需求，强调现有方法的局限性，如全量微调资源密集，以及像低秩适应（LoRA）这样的参数高效方法在安全一致性上的妥协。提出的NeST（神经元选择性调优）框架通过选择性调优通过激活探测识别的与安全相关的神经元，提供了一种新颖的解决方案，实现高效的后期安全对齐，而无需修改整个模型。该方法的动机在于需要一种稳健且可维护的安全方法，最大限度地减少计算开销，同时最大化有效性。NeST通过在各种模型中显著降低越狱攻击成功率，做出了重要贡献，在仅训练少量参数的情况下，文本模型的成功率从44.5%降至1.1%，多模态设置的成功率从55.3%降至1.1%，从而支持其高效安全对齐的目标。
Culturally-Adapted Red-Teaming Across East and Southeast Asian Contexts: A Methodological and Comparative Analysis
Authors: Hyeji Choi, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-06-08T08:17:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-08T08:17:18+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICML 2026 Workshop on AIWILDS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multilingual safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) has predominantly relied on direct translation (DT) of English benchmarks into target languages - an approach that converts surface-level linguistic form while failing to reflect the cultural context embedded in threat scenarios, social norms, and legal frameworks. We construct paired DT and culturally-adapted (CA) datasets via 1:1 seed matching for four languages - Korean (KO), Japanese (JA), Thai (TH), and Khmer (KM) - and compare Attack Success Rate (ASR) and Cultural Realism scores across four open-source LLM. CA prompts yield Delta-ASR > 0 across all 16 language x model combinations (mean +9.3 pp), and DT-based evaluation underestimates risk in 44 of 48 category x language combinations. Language-level analysis reveals that the distribution of threat forms is heterogeneous across languages. Cultural Realism analysis further shows that DT Cultural Depth (C3) scores remain consistently below 1.0 out of 3.0 across all four languages (mean 0.17), whereas CA scores reach up to 2.51, indicating that direct translation produces inputs systematically divergent from those encountered in real-world multicultural settings. These findings demonstrate that adapting benchmarks to language-specific cultural contexts - rather than relying on linguistic translation alone - is necessary for valid multilingual LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：跨东亚和东南亚背景的文化适应性红队：方法论和比较分析
大型语言模型（LLMs）的多语言安全评估主要依赖于将英语基准直接翻译（DT）为目标语言，这种方法仅转换表层语言形式，未能反映威胁场景、社会规范和法律框架中嵌入的文化背景。我们通过1:1种子匹配构建了四种语言（韩语、日语、泰语和高棉语）的配对DT和文化适应（CA）数据集，并比较了四个开源LLM的攻击成功率（ASR）和文化现实评分。CA提示在所有16种语言x模型组合中产生Delta-ASR > 0（平均+9.3个百分点），而基于DT的评估在48个类别x语言组合中低估了风险。语言级分析显示，威胁形式的分布在不同语言中是异质的。文化现实分析进一步表明，DT文化深度（C3）评分在所有四种语言中始终低于3.0的1.0（平均0.17），而CA评分高达2.51，表明直接翻译产生的输入与现实世界多文化环境中遇到的输入系统性偏离。这些发现表明，适应特定语言文化背景的基准，而不仅仅依赖语言翻译，对于有效的多语言LLM安全评估是必要的。

When Behavioral Safety Evaluation Fails: A Representation-Level Perspective
Authors: Enyi Jiang, Anders Gjølbye, Yibo Jacky Zhang, Sanmi Koyejo
First: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) safety has often been evaluated at the behavior level, which provides limited evidence of internal robustness, as these evaluations target outputs rather than representation-level vulnerability under intervention. We formalize this discrepancy as the audit gap: the difference between behavioral safety and robustness under intervention. To study this gap, we construct dissociated models that preserve safe outward behavior while remaining vulnerable in the latent space. We introduce an intervention-based evaluation framework to test model robustness through soft interventions in parameter and latent spaces, including harmful fine-tuning and layer-wise latent perturbations. To formalize the evaluation, we propose the Latent Vulnerability Score (LVS) to measure how easily harmful behavior can be elicited by bounded latent perturbations. Using this evaluation framework, we show that behavioral safety metrics are insufficient measures of representation-level robustness across multiple safely and unsafely aligned state-of-the-art models. Notably, dissociated models show substantially elevated LVSs despite comparable refusal behavior under harmful intervention, with intermediate representations being the most sensitive to intervention. Our results suggest that behavioral safety evaluation alone provides an incomplete picture of model robustness, motivating representation-aware audits of latent vulnerability and observable behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：行为安全评估失败时：一种表征层面的视角
大型语言模型（LLM）的安全性通常在行为层面进行评估，这提供了有限的内部稳健性证据，因为这些评估针对的是输出，而不是干预下的表征层面脆弱性。我们将这种差异形式化为审计差距：行为安全与干预下的稳健性之间的差异。为了研究这一差距，我们构建了保持安全外部行为的分离模型，同时在潜在空间中保持脆弱性。我们引入了一种基于干预的评估框架，通过参数和潜在空间中的软干预来测试模型的稳健性，包括有害的微调和层级潜在扰动。为了形式化评估，我们提出了潜在脆弱性评分（LVS），以测量有害行为在有限潜在扰动下被引发的难易程度。使用该评估框架，我们表明行为安全指标不足以衡量多种安全和不安全对齐的最先进模型的表征层面稳健性。值得注意的是，尽管在有害干预下拒绝行为相当，分离模型的LVS显著升高，中间表征对干预最为敏感。我们的结果表明，仅依靠行为安全评估无法全面反映模型的稳健性，促使对潜在脆弱性和可观察行为进行表征意识审计。

PreAct-Bench: Benchmarking Predictive Monitoring in LLMs
Authors: Hainiu Xu, Italo Luis da Silva, Jiangnan Ye, Yuhao Wang, Wei Liu, Linyi Yang, Jonathan Richard Schwarz, Nicola Paoletti, Yulan He, Hanqi Yan
First: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PreAct-Bench：大语言模型预测监控基准测试
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被部署为能够执行多步骤行动轨迹以实现特定目标的自主代理。虽然现有的安全研究集中在检测完整轨迹中的不道德行为，但这种范式在根本上是回顾性的：它仅在伤害发生后识别出伤害。在本研究中，我们研究了一个关键但被忽视的安全任务，我们称之为预测监控：仅给定部分行动轨迹，模型能否推断出在显性行动执行之前它是否会以不道德行为告终？为了支持这一任务，我们提出了PreAct-Bench，这是一个涵盖五个领域的1,000对伦理和不伦理行动轨迹的基准测试。我们使用我们的Prefix Foresight F1指标评估了一系列LLMs、安全护栏模型和潜在探测方法在不同的行动轨迹分数下的表现。结果表明，尽管人类表现出良好的性能，但即使对于强模型，预测监控仍然具有挑战性，突显了LLM安全中未来导向风险推理的必要性。

This paper introduces a novel approach called Predictive Monitoring, which aims to assess the potential for unethical actions based on partial action trajectories. The authors present PreAct-Bench, a benchmark consisting of 1,000 ethical and unethical action trajectory pairs across five domains, and evaluate various LLMs and safety models using the Prefix Foresight F1 metric. The findings indicate that while human performance is promising, predictive monitoring remains a significant challenge for even advanced models, underscoring the necessity for proactive risk assessment in LLM safety.

TamperBench: Systematically Stress-Testing LLM Safety Under Fine-Tuning and Tampering
Authors: Saad Hossain, Tom Tseng, Punya Syon Pandey, Samanvay Vajpayee, Matthew Kowal, Nayeema Nonta, Samuel Simko, Stephen Casper, Zhijing Jin, Kellin Pelrine, Sirisha Rambhatla
First: 2026-02-06T18:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T23:27:30+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 15 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As increasingly capable open-weight large language models (LLMs) are deployed, improving their tamper resistance against unsafe modifications, whether accidental or intentional, becomes critical to minimize risks. However, there is no standard approach to evaluate tamper resistance. Varied datasets, metrics, and tampering configurations make it difficult to compare safety, utility, and robustness across different models and defenses. To address this, we introduce TamperBench, the first unified framework to systematically evaluate the tamper resistance of LLMs. TamperBench (i) curates a repository of state-of-the-art weight-space fine-tuning attacks, latent-space representation attacks, and alignment-stage defenses; (ii) enables realistic adversarial evaluation through systematic hyperparameter sweeps per attack-model pair; and (iii) provides both safety and utility evaluations. We use TamperBench to evaluate 21 open-weight LLMs, including defense-augmented variants, across nine tampering threats using standardized safety and capability metrics with hyperparameter sweeps per model-attack pair. The results provide insights including effects of post-training on tamper resistance, that jailbreak-tuning is typically the most severe attack, and that current alignment-stage defenses largely fail to withstand attack sweeps. Code is available at https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TamperBench：系统性压力测试LLM在微调和篡改下的安全性
随着越来越强大的开放权重大型语言模型（LLM）的部署，提高其对不安全修改（无论是意外还是故意）的抗篡改能力变得至关重要，以最小化风险。然而，目前没有标准的方法来评估抗篡改能力。不同的数据集、指标和篡改配置使得比较不同模型和防御的安全性、实用性和鲁棒性变得困难。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了TamperBench，这是第一个统一框架，用于系统性评估LLM的抗篡改能力。TamperBench (i) 收集了最先进的权重空间微调攻击、潜在空间表示攻击和对齐阶段防御的库；(ii) 通过对每个攻击-模型对进行系统的超参数搜索，实现现实的对抗性评估；(iii) 提供安全性和实用性评估。我们使用TamperBench评估了21个开放权重LLM，包括增强防御的变体，针对九种篡改威胁使用标准化的安全性和能力指标，并对每个模型-攻击对进行超参数搜索。结果提供了包括后训练对抗篡改能力的影响、越狱微调通常是最严重的攻击，以及当前对齐阶段防御在抵御攻击时大多失败的见解。代码可在https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for improving tamper resistance in large language models (LLMs) as their deployment increases, highlighting the lack of standardized methods for evaluating this resistance. Previous approaches have been hindered by inconsistent datasets, metrics, and configurations, making it challenging to compare safety and robustness across models. The proposed TamperBench framework overcomes these issues by providing a unified system to evaluate LLM tamper resistance through curated attacks and systematic hyperparameter sweeps, enabling both safety and utility assessments. This paper contributes by evaluating 21 open-weight LLMs against nine tampering threats, revealing that post-training effects significantly influence tamper resistance and that existing defenses often fail under attack conditions. The methodology demonstrates effective performance in assessing LLM safety, supporting the goal of enhancing model robustness against tampering.
本研究解决了随着大型语言模型（LLMs）部署增加而对其抗篡改能力评估的迫切需求，强调了缺乏标准化评估方法的问题。以往的方法受到不一致的数据集、指标和配置的限制，使得不同模型之间的比较变得困难。提出的TamperBench框架通过提供一个统一的系统，系统地评估LLM的抗篡改能力，通过策划的攻击和防御，能够通过超参数搜索进行现实的评估。本文的贡献在于引入了一个全面的攻击和防御库，并对21个LLM在九种篡改威胁下进行了评估，揭示了后训练效果显著影响抗篡改能力，现有防御通常不足。该方法论表明，TamperBench能够有效评估安全性和实用性，支持其增强LLM抗篡改能力的目标。
When Autoregressive Consistency Hurts Safety Alignment
Authors: Bochen Lyu, Yiyang Jia, Xiaohao Cai, Zhanxing Zhu
First: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00
Comments: 21 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment in large language models (LLMs) is fragile in part because it is often shallow: fine-tuning mainly reshapes the model's behavior near the first few output tokens. We argue that this phenomenon can be understood through autoregressive consistency, the tendency of next-token prediction to preserve and extend the current response trajectory consistently. By analyzing the learning dynamics of safety alignment, we show that autoregressive consistency can concentrate alignment updates on early tokens, offering a mechanistic explanation for shallow safety alignment. The same mechanism also predicts a broader class of attacks on LLMs: attacks that induce harmful continuation states at arbitrary positions in the output trajectory. As a concrete example, we introduce random insertion attack, which inserts a short harmful span into an otherwise safe refusal trajectory and exploits autoregressive consistency to sustain the resulting harmful branch, thereby bypassing safety alignment. Notably, a short harmful span can redirect the generation to be harmful even after a long refusal prefix, highlighting autoregressive consistency as a potential broader failure mechanism. This suggests that safety alignment should also break harmful autoregressive consistency throughout the output trajectory. We therefore propose adversarial safety alignment, an initial framework based on worst-case harmful continuation states, and instantiate it with random worst-insertion training. Overall, our results suggest that autoregressive consistency should be treated as a central consideration in both safety alignment and attack design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归一致性如何损害安全对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐脆弱，部分原因在于其通常较浅：微调主要重塑模型在前几个输出标记附近的行为。我们认为，这一现象可以通过自回归一致性来理解，即下一个标记预测保持并延续当前响应轨迹的一致性倾向。通过分析安全对齐的学习动态，我们表明自回归一致性可以将对齐更新集中在早期标记上，为浅层安全对齐提供了机制性解释。同样的机制也预测了一类更广泛的对LLMs的攻击：在输出轨迹的任意位置诱导有害延续状态的攻击。作为具体例子，我们引入随机插入攻击，该攻击将一个短的有害片段插入到原本安全的拒绝轨迹中，并利用自回归一致性来维持由此产生的有害分支，从而绕过安全对齐。值得注意的是，一个短的有害片段可以在长拒绝前缀后重新引导生成变得有害，突显自回归一致性作为潜在的更广泛失败机制。这表明安全对齐也应打破输出轨迹中有害的自回归一致性。因此，我们提出了对抗性安全对齐，这是一个基于最坏情况有害延续状态的初步框架，并通过随机最坏插入训练进行实例化。总体而言，我们的结果表明，自回归一致性应被视为安全对齐和攻击设计中的核心考虑。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragility of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which is often shallow due to fine-tuning primarily affecting the initial output tokens. Previous methods have struggled with this issue, as they tend to focus on early tokens, leading to vulnerabilities in safety alignment. The proposed approach, adversarial safety alignment, aims to mitigate these weaknesses by considering harmful continuation states throughout the entire output trajectory, rather than just the beginning. This methodology includes random worst-insertion training to enhance safety alignment against potential attacks. The findings indicate that autoregressive consistency can lead to harmful outputs even after safe prefixes, demonstrating the need for a more robust safety alignment framework that effectively addresses these risks.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全对齐的脆弱性，这种脆弱性往往是由于微调主要影响初始输出标记而导致的。以往的方法虽然致力于增强安全对齐，但未能充分解决自回归一致性的问题，这可能导致输出中的有害延续状态。提出的方法，即对抗性安全对齐，旨在通过考虑最坏情况下的有害延续状态并采用随机最坏插入训练来减轻这些风险。这一方法论表明，自回归一致性在安全对齐和潜在攻击中可能是一个重要因素，实验结果表明，新框架能够有效地在安全拒绝后重新引导有害输出，从而支持在整个输出轨迹中需要更强健的安全对齐策略。
Black-box, Adaptive, Efficient, Transferable, Harmful, Applicable... Attacks Are All You Need to Break LLMs
Authors: Vincent Limbach, Jonas Dornbusch, David Lüdke, Stephan Günnemann, Leo Schwinn
First: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurately evaluating adversarial robustness is a longstanding challenge. A flawed attack design can inflate robustness estimates, making deployment risk assessment and defense comparison unreliable. Historically, standardized attacks such as AutoAttack have largely resolved this for image classifiers, providing a reliable evaluation baseline for systematic comparison across defenses. However, no equivalent exists for LLM jailbreak evaluation yet, where designing such an attack is considerably more difficult. A reliable attack must, among other things, be black-box compatible, applicable to arbitrary defense pipelines, and efficient, which no existing method jointly satisfies. We introduce Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), a masked diffusion language model attacker trained via iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, requiring only black-box access to the target. The same method can be used without modification as a strong adaptive attack on individual behaviors, or as an efficient amortized policy that transfers to held-out behaviors and unseen target models without fine-tuning. Even against layered defenses, such as a Circuit Breaker-trained model combined with an auxiliary detector, IHO improves attack success considerably over state-of-the-art approaches, without any defense-specific adaptation. Our results position IHO as a practical step toward the kind of standardized jailbreak evaluation that has improved reliability in the past. Code and models are available on GitHub and Hugging Face.
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑箱、自适应、高效、可转移、有害、适用……攻击是破解大型语言模型所需的一切
准确评估对抗鲁棒性一直是一个长期挑战。设计不当的攻击可能会夸大鲁棒性估计，使得部署风险评估和防御比较不可靠。历史上，标准化攻击如AutoAttack在图像分类器中基本解决了这一问题，为系统比较提供了可靠的评估基准。然而，目前尚无等效的LLM越狱评估标准，设计这样的攻击要困难得多。一个可靠的攻击必须在许多方面兼容黑箱，适用于任意防御管道，并且高效，而现有方法没有一个能够共同满足这些要求。我们引入了间接有害优化（IHO），这是一种通过迭代偏好优化训练的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者，仅需对目标进行黑箱访问。相同的方法可以在不修改的情况下作为对个体行为的强自适应攻击，或作为一种高效的摊销策略，能够转移到未见的目标模型和保留行为上，而无需微调。即使面对分层防御，如与辅助检测器结合的电路断路器训练模型，IHO在攻击成功率上显著超越了最先进的方法，而无需任何特定于防御的适应。我们的结果将IHO定位为朝着标准化越狱评估的实用步骤，这在过去提高了可靠性。代码和模型可在GitHub和Hugging Face上获取。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the challenge of accurately evaluating the adversarial robustness of large language models (LLMs), highlighting the inadequacies of existing attack designs that inflate robustness estimates and compromise risk assessments. Previous methods, such as standardized attacks for image classifiers, lack a reliable equivalent for LLM jailbreak evaluations, primarily due to the complexity of designing effective attacks that are black-box compatible and applicable across various defense mechanisms. The proposed approach, Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), utilizes a masked diffusion language model trained through iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, allowing it to function as both a strong adaptive attack and an efficient policy for transferring to unseen models without fine-tuning. The methodology demonstrates significant improvements in attack success rates against layered defenses compared to state-of-the-art methods, thereby contributing to the establishment of standardized evaluation practices for LLMs, which enhances the reliability of robustness assessments.
本研究解决了准确评估大型语言模型（LLMs）对抗鲁棒性的问题，强调现有的图像分类器标准化攻击方法无法有效转化为LLMs，因为攻击设计的复杂性。以往的方法在提供可靠评估方面存在困难，通常缺乏黑箱兼容性、效率和适用于各种防御机制的能力。所提出的方法间接危害优化（IHO）通过利用仅需黑箱访问的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者，克服了这些局限性，并且能够在不同行为之间适应而无需微调。本文贡献了一种新颖的方法论，与最先进的技术相比，显著提高了对分层防御的攻击成功率，从而推动了LLMs的越狱评估的可靠性，并支持了标准化评估框架的需求。
D-Judge: Disrupting Multi-Turn Jailbreaks using Semantics-Preserving Output Rewriting
Authors: Huanli Gong, Zhipeng Wei, Yu Fu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Ananya Gupta, Yue Dong, N. Benjamin Erichson
First: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 43rd International Conference on Machine Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks pose a growing threat to large language model (LLM) safety because they exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to iteratively refine prompts toward harmful goals. Existing defenses largely detect or block unsafe content at individual turns or at the final response, leaving the judge-driven refinement loop intact and allowing attackers to extract informative feedback from intermediate interactions. We introduce D-Judge, a semantics-preserving output rewriting defense that intervenes directly in this loop by rewriting the victim LLM's responses before they are evaluated by the attacker's judge. By misaligning the judge's feedback signal without changing the meaning of the original response, D-Judge derails the attacker's prompt-refinement process, causing subsequent queries to be optimized against a distorted signal of attack progress. To improve D-Judge's ability to produce such rewrites, we construct a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs that induce different judge-assigned harmfulness scores, and use it for supervised fine-tuning followed by direct preference optimization. Experiments on HarmBench show that D-Judge reduces the success rate of state-of-the-art multi-turn jailbreaks while preserving performance on benign benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：D-Judge：通过语义保持输出重写来破坏多轮越狱攻击
多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）的安全构成日益严重的威胁，因为它们利用辅助评判模型的反馈，迭代地优化提示以达到有害目标。现有防御主要在单个回合或最终响应中检测或阻止不安全内容，保持评判驱动的优化循环不变，使攻击者能够从中间交互中提取有用反馈。我们提出D-Judge，一种语义保持输出重写防御，直接干预这一循环，通过在攻击者的评判之前重写受害者LLM的响应。通过在不改变原始响应含义的情况下使评判的反馈信号失真，D-Judge使攻击者的提示优化过程偏离轨道，导致后续查询针对扭曲的攻击进展信号进行优化。为了提高D-Judge生成此类重写的能力，我们构建了一个语义等价响应对的数据集，该数据集引发不同的评判分配有害性评分，并用于监督微调，随后进行直接偏好优化。在HarmBench上的实验表明，D-Judge在保持良性基准性能的同时，降低了最先进的多轮越狱攻击的成功率。

Previous methods primarily focused on detecting or blocking unsafe content but failed to disrupt the iterative feedback loop that attackers exploit. The proposed approach, D-Judge, intervenes directly in this loop by rewriting the LLM's responses before they are evaluated by the judge, thus misaligning the feedback signal while preserving the original meaning. This method is well-motivated as it targets the core of the attack mechanism. The contribution of the paper lies in the development of a dataset for supervised fine-tuning that enhances D-Judge's ability to produce effective rewrites. Experiments conducted on HarmBench demonstrate that D-Judge significantly reduces the success rate of advanced multi-turn jailbreaks while maintaining performance on benign tasks.

Quality-Diversity Evolution for Discovering Diverse Vulnerabilities in LLM Safety
Authors: Subhadip Mitra
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 6 figures. Accepted at the ICLR 2026 Workshop on Agents in the Wild (AIWILD)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Current approaches to LLM adversarial testing suffer from coverage gaps: manual red-teaming does not scale, LLM-as-attacker methods exhibit mode collapse, and gradient-based approaches produce uninterpretable gibberish. We introduce a quality-diversity evolutionary framework that operates at the semantic level, evolving interpretable attack strategies rather than token sequences. Using MAP-Elites, we maintain a diverse archive of attacks across behavioral dimensions (strategy type, encoding method, prompt length). In experiments across GPT-4o-mini, Claude 3.5 Sonnet, Gemini 2.0 Flash, and an open-weight coding model (Devstral-small-2), we discover distinct vulnerability profiles: GPT-4o-mini is vulnerable to hypothetical and multi-turn framing combined with ROT13 encoding (fitness 0.8), Gemini to direct attacks with ROT13 and multi-turn with Leetspeak (0.8), while Claude shows uniformly ambiguous responses across all strategies (max 0.4). The semantic representation produces interpretable attacks that reveal systematic, model-specific weaknesses, providing actionable insights for improving LLM safety and a reproducible baseline for evaluating future frontier models. Code and experiment artifacts are released at https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于发现LLM安全性中多样化脆弱性的质量-多样性进化
当前LLM对抗测试的方法存在覆盖缺口：手动红队无法扩展，LLM作为攻击者的方法表现出模式崩溃，基于梯度的方法产生不可解释的乱码。我们引入了一种在语义层面上操作的质量-多样性进化框架，进化可解释的攻击策略而非令牌序列。使用MAP-Elites，我们维护一个跨行为维度（策略类型、编码方法、提示长度）的多样化攻击档案。在对GPT-4o-mini、Claude 3.5 Sonnet、Gemini 2.0 Flash和一个开放权重编码模型（Devstral-small-2）的实验中，我们发现了不同的脆弱性特征：GPT-4o-mini对假设性和多轮框架结合ROT13编码（适应度0.8）脆弱，Gemini对直接攻击使用ROT13和多轮使用Leetspeak（0.8）脆弱，而Claude在所有策略中表现出均匀模糊的响应（最大0.4）。语义表示产生可解释的攻击，揭示系统性、模型特定的弱点，为改善LLM安全性提供可操作的见解，并为评估未来前沿模型提供可重复的基线。代码和实验文物已发布在https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen。

The Refusal--Compliance Tradeoff: A Large-Scale Safety Behavior Audit of Large Language Models
Authors: Alif Al Hasan, Sumon Biswas
First: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T15:07:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Refusal rates are a poor proxy for LLM safety, i.e., a model may over-refuse benign prompts while still complying with harmful ones. We audit both failure modes across 21 open-weight LLMs on four safety benchmarks (OR-Bench, XSTest, ToxiGen, BOLD), using a composition adjustment to isolate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity confounds. We report three findings. First, models adopt fundamentally different calibration strategies: conservative ecosystems such as Llama suppress unsafe outputs at the cost of elevated over-refusals, while permissive ecosystems such as DeepSeek and Qwen preserve helpfulness but tolerate higher harmful compliance. Second, demographic protection is unequal: models over-protect prominent racial and religious groups, frequently refusing even benign prompts about them, while providing substantially weaker protection against disability-targeted attacks. Third, refusal and compliance tendencies are stable within model families across generations and scales, suggesting that post-training objectives shape safety behavior more than architecture. Our results call for joint, demographically-aware, and multi-judge safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：拒绝与合规权衡：大规模语言模型的安全行为审计
拒绝率是大型语言模型安全性的不良代理，即模型可能在过度拒绝良性提示的同时仍然对有害提示做出响应。我们在四个安全基准（OR-Bench、XSTest、ToxiGen、BOLD）上审计了21个开放权重的LLM，使用组合调整来隔离模型敏感性与数据集毒性混淆。我们报告了三个发现。首先，模型采用根本不同的校准策略：保守生态系统如Llama在提高过度拒绝的代价下抑制不安全输出，而宽松生态系统如DeepSeek和Qwen则保持有用性但容忍更高的有害合规性。其次，人口保护不平等：模型过度保护显著的种族和宗教群体，频繁拒绝关于它们的良性提示，而对残疾目标攻击提供的保护则明显较弱。第三，拒绝和合规倾向在模型家族中跨代和规模保持稳定，表明后训练目标在塑造安全行为方面的影响大于架构。我们的结果呼吁进行联合、关注人口统计和多评审的安全评估。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the inadequacy of refusal rates as indicators of safety in large language models (LLMs), highlighting that models may refuse benign prompts while complying with harmful ones. Previous methods primarily focused on refusal rates without considering the nuances of model behavior, leading to misleading assessments of safety. The proposed approach involves a comprehensive audit of 21 open-weight LLMs across four safety benchmarks, utilizing a composition adjustment to differentiate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity. The paper contributes by revealing distinct calibration strategies among models, demonstrating unequal demographic protection, and showing that refusal and compliance tendencies are consistent within model families. The methodology effectively assesses safety behavior, achieving insights that support the need for more nuanced and equitable safety evaluations in LLMs.
本文探讨了拒绝率作为大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性指标的不足，强调模型可能拒绝良性提示而对有害内容却表示遵从。以往的方法主要集中在拒绝率上，未考虑模型行为的细微差别，导致安全性评估误导。提出的方法涉及对21个开放权重LLM在四个安全基准上的大规模审计，利用组成调整来区分模型敏感性与数据集毒性。该方法揭示了模型表现出不同的校准策略，保守模型如Llama优先考虑安全性，但导致过度拒绝，而宽容模型如DeepSeek则保持有用性，但允许有害的遵从。研究结果表明，人口保护不平等，并且安全行为更多地受后训练目标的影响，而非模型架构，促使对更全面和考虑人口因素的安全评估的呼吁。
How Reliable Are AI Attackers Against a Fixed Vulnerable Target? A 400-Run Empirical Study of LLM Penetration Testing Consistency
Authors: Galip Tolga Erdem
First: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00
Comments: 41 pages, 7 figures. Code and 400-run dataset: https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20421592
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can autonomously conduct multi-stage cyber attacks, but the consistency of their offensive behavior under repeated trials remains unstudied. This work presents the first large-scale empirical measurement of LLM attack consistency: 400 autonomous penetration testing runs (4 models, 100 each) against an identical honeypot hosting OWASP Juice Shop and two additional vulnerable services, holding prompt, orchestrator, and target constant. No model emitted a content refusal that survived the orchestrator's one-shot authorization re-prompt at iterations 0-1. Claude Sonnet 4's API calls did encounter upstream service unavailability - 91 of 1,135 calls returned HTTP 529 overloaded_error during a documented Anthropic capacity event, truncating 39 of 100 Claude runs. An earlier draft catalogued these as safety refusals; on full-log audit they are upstream API failures, not model-level refusals. Despite this, Claude achieved full exploitation in 61 of 100 runs; Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85; GPT-4o-mini in 56 while deploying 98 unique attack strategies; qwen2.5-coder:14b in 25. Failure modes are model-distinctive: Claude through API truncation (39 runs), qwen through premature completion (52), GPT-4o-mini through iteration-budget exhaustion (23). Cross-service credential reuse appeared only in configurations retaining the most conversation history (qwen 57%, GPT-4o-mini 49%, cloud models 0% on 5-exchange windows). Cross-model exploitation rate differences are statistically significant (p < 0.001) with large effect sizes; qwen vs. Gemini SQL injection rates differ at Cohen's h = 1.12. First-exploit timing fell within a 15-30 second wall-clock range. To our knowledge, this is the first study to measure autonomous LLM attack behavior at N=100 per model across a multi-service target.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI攻击者对固定脆弱目标的可靠性如何？一项400次运行的LLM渗透测试一致性实证研究
大型语言模型（LLMs）可以自主进行多阶段网络攻击，但其在重复试验中的攻击行为一致性尚未研究。本研究首次大规模实证测量LLM攻击一致性：对一个托管OWASP Juice Shop和两个额外脆弱服务的相同蜜罐进行400次自主渗透测试（4个模型，各100次），保持提示、协调者和目标不变。在迭代0-1中，没有模型发出经过协调者一次性授权重新提示后仍然有效的内容拒绝。Claude Sonnet 4的API调用确实遇到了上游服务不可用的情况——在一次记录的Anthropic容量事件中，1,135次调用中有91次返回HTTP 529 overloaded_error，导致100次Claude运行中有39次被截断。早期草稿将这些列为安全拒绝；经过完整日志审计后，它们被认定为上游API故障，而非模型级拒绝。尽管如此，Claude在100次运行中实现了61次完全利用；Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite实现了85次；GPT-4o-mini实现了56次，同时部署了98种独特的攻击策略；qwen2.5-coder:14b实现了25次。失败模式具有模型特征：Claude通过API截断（39次运行），qwen通过过早完成（52次），GPT-4o-mini通过迭代预算耗尽（23次）。跨服务凭证重用仅出现在保留最多对话历史的配置中（qwen 57%，GPT-4o-mini 49%，云模型在5次交换窗口中为0%）。跨模型利用率差异具有统计显著性（p < 0.001），且效应量大；qwen与Gemini的SQL注入率差异为Cohen's h = 1.12。首次利用的时间落在15-30秒的实际时间范围内。据我们所知，这是首个在多服务目标上测量自主LLM攻击行为的研究，每个模型N=100。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the consistency of offensive behavior exhibited by large language models (LLMs) during autonomous cyber attacks, a topic that has not been extensively studied despite the increasing use of LLMs for penetration testing. Previous methods lacked comprehensive empirical measurement and did not account for the variability in attack outcomes across multiple trials. The proposed approach involves conducting 400 penetration testing runs across four different models against a consistent honeypot setup, allowing for a detailed analysis of attack consistency and model performance. The study reveals significant differences in exploitation rates and failure modes among the models, with Claude achieving full exploitation in 61 out of 100 runs and Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85, indicating that the proposed methodology effectively captures the nuances of LLM attack behavior. The findings contribute to understanding LLM reliability in cybersecurity applications and highlight the importance of model selection in penetration testing scenarios.

Beyond Attack Success Rate: Temporal Logit Observability for LLM Safety Failures
Authors: Junyoung Park, Sunghwan Park, Seongyong Ju, Jaewoo Lee
First: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Attack Success Rate (ASR) evaluates each jailbreak with a single yes/no label at the end of generation, telling us whether a failure happened but not how it unfolded. Two attacks that produce equally harmful outputs may have followed completely different paths, and ASR cannot tell them apart. We make those hidden paths observable from logits alone. Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) is a training-free diagnostic that watches a compliance-refusal margin during decoding and places each model-attack condition on a calibrated 2D plane. By design, this plane is most informative exactly where ASR is least informative: among attacks that succeed for genuinely different reasons. Across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, attacks with nearly identical ASR land at clearly different points on the plane: the same model can fail through different temporal patterns. The geometry matches refusal-direction probes from hidden states on most conditions, with one model showing the limit of our fixed-lexicon approach. A simple early-stop rule derived from TLO cuts successful jailbreaks by more than half, without false alarms on plain benign queries. Safety evaluation should report when and how a failure unfolds, not only whether it occurred. TLO makes the first two observable from logits alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越攻击成功率：LLM安全失败的时间逻辑可观察性
攻击成功率（ASR）在生成结束时用单一的是/否标签评估每个越狱，告诉我们是否发生了失败，但不说明其如何展开。两个产生同样有害输出的攻击可能遵循完全不同的路径，而ASR无法区分它们。我们使这些隐藏路径仅通过逻辑可观察。时间逻辑可观察性（TLO）是一种无训练的诊断方法，在解码过程中观察合规-拒绝边际，并将每个模型-攻击条件放置在一个校准的二维平面上。根据设计，这个平面在ASR信息最少的地方最具信息性：在因真正不同原因而成功的攻击之间。在四个对齐的LLM和三种越狱范式中，攻击几乎相同的ASR在平面上明显不同的点上：同一模型可以通过不同的时间模式失败。几何形状与大多数条件下隐藏状态的拒绝方向探测相匹配，其中一个模型显示了我们固定词汇表方法的极限。基于TLO的简单早停规则将成功的越狱减少了一半以上，而在普通良性查询上没有误报。安全评估应报告失败何时以及如何展开，而不仅仅是是否发生。TLO使前两者仅通过逻辑可观察。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of the Attack Success Rate (ASR) metric, which only indicates whether a failure occurred without revealing the underlying processes. Previous methods have relied on ASR, which fails to differentiate between attacks that yield similar harmful outputs but follow different paths. The proposed approach, Temporal Logit Observability (TLO), offers a training-free diagnostic tool that visualizes the compliance-refusal margin during decoding on a calibrated 2D plane, providing insights into the distinct paths of attacks. This method is well-motivated as it enhances the understanding of LLM safety failures by revealing the temporal patterns of attacks. The study demonstrates that TLO can effectively differentiate between attacks with identical ASR across multiple LLMs and jailbreak paradigms, leading to a significant reduction in successful jailbreaks by over 50% without generating false alarms on benign queries, thus supporting the goal of improving safety evaluations in LLMs.
本研究解决了攻击成功率（ASR）指标的局限性，该指标仅指示大型语言模型（LLMs）上的越狱攻击是否成功，而未提供潜在过程的见解。传统方法，包括ASR，无法区分产生相似有害输出但遵循不同路径的攻击，导致对模型脆弱性的理解不足。提出的方法，时间逻辑可观察性（TLO），提供了一种无训练的诊断方法，通过可视化解码过程中的合规-拒绝边际，允许对攻击行为进行更细致的分析。该方法的贡献在于揭示了不同攻击可以因不同原因而成功的方式，研究表明在四个LLM和三种越狱范式中，具有相同ASR的攻击在经过校准的二维平面上表现出不同的模式。研究结果表明，基于TLO实施的简单早停规则可以将成功的越狱攻击减少超过50%，而不会在良性查询上产生误报，从而通过关注失败的动态而不仅仅是结果，增强了安全评估。
Aligned but Fragile: Enhancing LLM Safety Robustness via Zeroth-Order Optimization
Authors: Zhihao Liu, Yifan Wu, Jian Lou, Di Wang, Yuxi Zhou, Yuke Hu
First: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment for large language models (LLMs) aims to reduce harmful or unsafe behavior while preserving general utility. However, recent findings reveal that alignment effects can be fragile: lightweight post-alignment manipulations, such as parameter noise, activation noise, or quantization, can easily weaken the intended safety behavior. Prior efforts to improve robustness have primarily focused on data curation, modified alignment objectives, and safety-critical parameter identification, leaving the role of the optimizer itself largely unexplored. In this paper, we are the first to study the robustness of safety alignment from the perspective of the base optimizer. This optimizer-centric view naturally points to zeroth-order optimization, which provides a robustness-oriented signal by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. Based on this insight, we propose a hybrid framework that first performs standard first-order safety alignment and then applies zeroth-order refinement to improve robustness. Both theoretically and empirically, we show that only a few zeroth-order refinement steps can enhance robustness while preserving safety alignment. We further improve the efficiency of zeroth-order refinement by exploiting its inherent perturbation-based evaluations to estimate layer-wise robustness sensitivity, enabling the refinement process to concentrate updates on robustness-critical layers with modest training overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐但脆弱：通过零阶优化增强大型语言模型的安全性鲁棒性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐旨在减少有害或不安全行为，同时保持一般效用。然而，最近的研究发现，对齐效果可能是脆弱的：轻量级的后对齐操作，如参数噪声、激活噪声或量化，可能会轻易削弱预期的安全行为。以往提高鲁棒性的努力主要集中在数据策划、修改对齐目标和安全关键参数识别上，而优化器本身的作用则大多未被探索。 在本文中，我们首次从基础优化器的角度研究安全对齐的鲁棒性。这种以优化器为中心的视角自然指向零阶优化，它通过在扰动下评估安全对齐提供了一个面向鲁棒性的信号。基于这一见解，我们提出了一个混合框架，首先执行标准的一阶安全对齐，然后应用零阶精炼以提高鲁棒性。我们理论和实证地表明，仅需少量零阶精炼步骤即可在保持安全对齐的同时增强鲁棒性。我们进一步通过利用零阶精炼固有的基于扰动的评估来估计层级鲁棒性敏感性，提高了零阶精炼的效率，使精炼过程能够将更新集中在鲁棒性关键层上，且训练开销适中。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which aims to mitigate harmful behaviors while maintaining overall utility. Previous methods have primarily focused on data curation and modified alignment objectives, but they often overlook the role of the optimizer, leading to fragile safety behaviors under perturbations. This paper proposes a novel approach that centers on zeroth-order optimization to enhance robustness by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. The methodology involves a hybrid framework that combines standard first-order safety alignment with zeroth-order refinement, demonstrating that minimal refinement steps can significantly improve robustness without compromising safety alignment. The experimental results indicate that this approach effectively enhances robustness while maintaining safety, thus supporting the goals of improving LLM safety.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）安全对齐的脆弱性，轻量级操作可能会削弱预期的安全行为。以往的方法主要集中在数据整理和修改对齐目标上，忽视了优化器的作用，而本文旨在探讨这一点。提出的方法引入了一种混合框架，将标准的一阶安全对齐与零阶优化结合，以增强鲁棒性而不影响安全性。该方法论涉及在扰动下评估安全对齐，并通过少量零阶步骤进行精炼，显著提高鲁棒性，同时保持对齐。实验结果表明，该方法有效提高了LLMs的鲁棒性，支持了更安全模型行为的目标。
SelfGrader: LLM Jailbreak Detection via Anchored Token-Level Logits
Authors: Zikai Zhang, Rui Hu, Olivera Kotevska, Jiahao Xu
First: 2026-04-01T23:29:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools for answering user queries, yet they remain highly vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing guardrail methods typically rely on internal features or textual responses to detect malicious queries, which either introduce substantial latency or suffer from randomness in text generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose SelfGrader, a lightweight guardrail method that formulates jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits. Specifically, SelfGrader evaluates the safety of a user query within a compact set of numerical tokens (NTs) (e.g., 0-9) and interprets their logit distribution as an internal safety signal. To align these signals with the target safety rubric, SelfGrader constructs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and introduces a dual-perspective scoring rule that considers both the maliciousness and benignness of the query, yielding a stable and interpretable score that reflects harmfulness and reduces the false positive rate simultaneously. Extensive experiments across diverse jailbreak benchmarks, adaptive attacks, benign prompt benchmarks, multiple LLMs, and state-of-the-art guardrail baselines demonstrate that SelfGrader achieves strong robustness with low false positive rates, memory overhead, and latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SelfGrader：通过锚定的令牌级逻辑进行LLM越狱检测
大型语言模型（LLMs）是回答用户查询的强大工具，但它们仍然高度易受越狱攻击。现有的防护方法通常依赖于内部特征或文本响应来检测恶意查询，这要么引入了显著的延迟，要么在文本生成中遭受随机性。为克服这些限制，我们提出了SelfGrader，这是一种轻量级的防护方法，将越狱检测公式化为使用锚定令牌级逻辑的数值评分问题。具体而言，SelfGrader在一组紧凑的数值令牌（NTs）（例如，0-9）中评估用户查询的安全性，并将其逻辑分布解释为内部安全信号。为了将这些信号与目标安全标准对齐，SelfGrader构建了可能近似正确指导的ICL锚定示例，并引入了一种双视角评分规则，考虑查询的恶意性和良性，从而产生一个稳定且可解释的分数，反映有害性并同时降低误报率。在多种越狱基准、适应性攻击、良性提示基准、多个LLM和最先进的防护基线上的广泛实验表明，SelfGrader在低误报率、内存开销和延迟方面实现了强大的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, highlighting the limitations of existing guardrail methods that rely on internal features or textual responses, which can introduce latency and randomness. The proposed method, SelfGrader, distinguishes itself by framing jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits, which allows for a more stable and interpretable assessment of query safety. Experimental results demonstrate that SelfGrader outperforms existing methods in terms of robustness, achieving low false positive rates and minimal latency across multiple benchmarks and LLMs.

Jailbreaking and Mitigation of Vulnerabilities in Large Language Models
Authors: Benji Peng, Hanxuan Chen, Keyu Chen, Qian Niu, Ziqian Bi, Ming Liu, Pohsun Feng, Tianyang Wang, Lawrence K. Q. Yan, Yizhu Wen, Yichao Zhang, Caitlyn Heqi Yin, Xinyuan Song, Riyang Bao, Jiacheng Shi
Venue: Eureka 1(1) (2026) 26-61
First: 2024-10-20T00:00:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-27T16:38:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed artificial intelligence by advancing natural language understanding and generation, enabling applications across fields beyond healthcare, software engineering, and conversational systems. Despite these advancements in the past few years, LLMs have shown considerable vulnerabilities, particularly to prompt injection and jailbreaking attacks. This review analyzes the state of research on these vulnerabilities and presents available defense strategies. We roughly categorize attack approaches into prompt-based, model-based, multimodal, and multilingual, covering techniques such as adversarial prompting, backdoor injections, and cross-modality exploits. We also review various defense mechanisms, including prompt filtering, transformation, alignment techniques, multi-agent defenses, and self-regulation, evaluating their strengths and shortcomings. We also discuss key metrics and benchmarks used to assess LLM safety and robustness, noting challenges like the quantification of attack success in interactive contexts and biases in existing datasets. Identifying current research gaps, we suggest future directions for resilient alignment strategies, advanced defenses against evolving attacks, automation of jailbreak detection, and consideration of ethical and societal impacts. This review emphasizes the need for continued research and cooperation within the AI community to enhance LLM security and ensure their safe deployment.
中文标题/摘要

Previous methods for mitigating these vulnerabilities, such as prompt filtering and transformation techniques, have shown limitations in effectiveness and adaptability to evolving threats. The proposed approach in this review categorizes attack methods and defense strategies, providing a comprehensive analysis of their strengths and weaknesses while identifying gaps in current research. The methodology includes a thorough evaluation of existing defense mechanisms and the introduction of future directions for enhancing LLM security, such as automated jailbreak detection and ethical considerations. The findings highlight the need for improved resilience in LLMs, with an emphasis on collaborative efforts within the AI community to ensure robust and safe deployment of these models.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在多种攻击（如提示注入和越狱）下的显著脆弱性，这对其在多个应用中的部署构成风险。以往的缓解方法，包括提示过滤和转换技术，显示出在有效性和适应性方面的局限性。本文提出对现有防御策略的全面回顾，同时识别当前研究中的空白，从而激发对改进对齐策略和先进防御的需求。该方法论涉及对攻击方法的分类和对防御机制的评估，从而深入了解其优缺点。研究结果强调了持续研究和合作以增强LLM安全性的必要性，最终支持在各个领域安全部署的目标。
Got a Secret? LLM Agents Can't Keep It: Evaluating Privacy in Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Aman Priyanshu, Supriti Vijay, Esha Pahwa
First: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM safety evaluations predominantly test models in isolation, yet deployed AI agents increasingly operate within persistent social environments alongside other agents. We introduce a Moltbook-style simulation platform where thousands of LLM agents interact across communities over a simulated month, and use it to evaluate privacy as a downstream safety concern under varying degrees of social pressure. We find that shifting from single turn to multi turn social evaluation amplifies privacy violations (CIMemories 19.95% to Ours 45.30% across OpenAI models), that leakage is socially contagious, with agents 8 times more likely to disclose sensitive information after observing a peer do so, and that explicit privacy instructions reduce but do not eliminate this effect, leaving leakage rates above 37.8% even with safeguards. Our findings suggest that static chat based safety benchmarks systematically underestimate risks in agentic deployment, and that social context alone is sufficient to elicit sensitive disclosures that single turn evaluations would never surface.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有秘密吗？LLM代理无法保密：多代理系统中的隐私评估
LLM安全评估主要在孤立环境中测试模型，但部署的AI代理越来越多地在持久的社交环境中与其他代理一起操作。我们引入了一种Moltbook风格的模拟平台，在该平台上，数千个LLM代理在模拟的一个月内跨社区互动，并利用它评估在不同社交压力下的隐私作为下游安全问题。我们发现，从单轮到多轮社交评估的转变会加剧隐私侵犯（CIMemories 19.95%到我们的模型45.30%），泄露是社交传染的，代理在观察到同伴泄露后泄露敏感信息的可能性增加8倍，并且明确的隐私指令虽然减少但并未消除这一影响，即使有保护措施，泄露率仍高于37.8%。我们的研究结果表明，静态基于聊天的安全基准系统性低估了代理部署中的风险，仅社交背景就足以引发敏感信息的披露，而单轮评估永远无法揭示这些信息。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of existing safety evaluations for large language models (LLMs), which typically assess models in isolation rather than in social environments where they interact with other agents. Previous methods fail to capture the dynamics of privacy violations in multi-agent contexts, leading to an underestimation of risks associated with deployed AI agents. This paper introduces a Moltbook-style simulation platform that allows thousands of LLM agents to interact over a simulated month, providing a more realistic evaluation of privacy concerns under social pressure. The study reveals that multi-turn social evaluations significantly increase privacy violations, with a notable rise in sensitive information disclosure influenced by peer behavior. The findings indicate that traditional safety benchmarks are insufficient and highlight the need for evaluations that account for social contexts, demonstrating that even with privacy instructions, leakage rates remain alarmingly high, thus supporting the need for improved safety measures in agentic deployments.

Evolving and Detecting Multi-Turn Deception using Geometric Signatures
Authors: Surender Suresh Kumar, Mary L. Cummings
First: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety defenses for large language models (LLMs) are typically trained and evaluated on single-turn prompts, yet real attacks often unfold as indirect, multi-turn probing. To defend against this more nuanced form of deception, we present a unified pipeline that generates realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets via multi-objective genetic prompt optimization with co-evolving mutation operators. We validate this dataset through a human study, which also revealed that early generations yielded the most convincing deception and practical constraints such as adherence filtering and ordering effects. Using this data, we were able to detect deceptive attempts to access prohibited information using simple, explainable geometric signals in embedding space coupled with a lightweight feed-forward classifier. Three geometric features (angular coverage, distance ratio, and linearity) augmented with pairwise similarity statistics led to a compact predictive model that achieved consistently high recall (0.89) across base, reworded, and truncated (three-turn) scenarios, with test-time F1 ranging from 0.74-0.86. The results support a central hypothesis that multi-turn deceptive intent leaves a stable geometric footprint that enables lightweight, transparent screening without expensive end-to-end training. We further discuss responsible uses, limitations, and paths toward larger, more diverse human-evaluated datasets. The primary contribution to artificial intelligence is the multi-objective evolutionary framework for prompt generation, and the engineering application is the deployment of a lightweight geometric detection system for LLM safety infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用几何特征演变和检测多轮欺骗
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全防御通常在单轮提示上进行训练和评估，但真实攻击往往以间接的多轮探测形式展开。为了防御这种更微妙的欺骗形式，我们提出了一个统一的流程，通过多目标遗传提示优化与共同演变的变异操作生成现实的多轮欺骗问题集。我们通过一项人类研究验证了该数据集，该研究还揭示了早期生成的欺骗最具说服力，以及遵循过滤和排序效应等实际限制。利用这些数据，我们能够使用简单、可解释的几何信号在嵌入空间中检测试图访问禁止信息的欺骗尝试，并结合轻量级前馈分类器。三个几何特征（角度覆盖、距离比和线性）与成对相似性统计相结合，形成了一个紧凑的预测模型，在基础、改写和截断（三轮）场景中实现了一致的高召回率（0.89），测试时F1值范围为0.74-0.86。结果支持一个核心假设，即多轮欺骗意图留下稳定的几何足迹，使得无需昂贵的端到端训练即可实现轻量、透明的筛选。我们进一步讨论了负责任的使用、局限性以及朝向更大、更具多样性的人类评估数据集的路径。对人工智能的主要贡献是用于提示生成的多目标进化框架，工程应用是为LLM安全基础设施部署轻量级几何检测系统。
Summary / 总结

Previous methods have struggled to effectively detect nuanced multi-turn deception, leading to the development of a unified pipeline that utilizes multi-objective genetic prompt optimization to generate realistic deceptive question sets. This approach is well-motivated as it aims to enhance detection capabilities by focusing on the geometric signatures left by deceptive interactions. The paper contributes a novel multi-objective evolutionary framework for prompt generation and a lightweight geometric detection system that employs simple geometric features to identify deceptive attempts. The proposed methodology achieved high recall rates (0.89) and F1 scores ranging from 0.74 to 0.86 across various scenarios, demonstrating its effectiveness in detecting multi-turn deception and supporting the hypothesis that such deception leaves a stable geometric footprint for screening.

$D^2$-Monitor: Dynamic Safety Monitoring for Diffusion LLMs via Hesitation-Aware Routing
Authors: Aoxi Liu, Yupeng Chen, James Oldfield, Guanzhe Hong, Junchi Yu, Baoyuan Wu, Philip Torr, Adel Bibi
First: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the emergence of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) as an alternative to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs), safety monitoring for D-LLMs remains largely unexplored. Unlike AR-LLMs, D-LLMs generate text through a multi-step denoising process, exposing intermediate hidden representations that may contain safety-relevant information unavailable in standard single-step monitoring setups. Motivated by the suitability of lightweight probes for always-on monitoring, we analyze which trajectory-level signals best indicate when such probes are likely to struggle. We find that the most informative signal is safety hesitation: intermediate hidden states repeatedly falling within a small margin of the probe's decision boundary. The number of such hesitation steps in D-LLM's trajectory predicts probe failure effectively, providing a proxy of sample difficulty. Building on this analysis, we propose $D^2$-Monitor, a bi-level safety monitor for D-LLMs. $D^2$-Monitor adopts a lightweight probe as an always-on monitor to jointly estimate hesitation and perform base classification. When the hesitation level exceeds a threshold, a more expressive but computationally heavier probe is activated. This dynamic routing mechanism allocates monitoring resources efficiently at test time. Evaluated on 3 datasets (WildguardMix, ToxicChat, OpenAI-Moderation) across 4 D-LLMs, $D^2$-Monitor achieves state-of-the-art performance with a compact parameter footprint ($\leq$ 0.85M parameters), and exhibits the best trade-off between effectiveness and efficiency relative to 8 baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$D^2$-监控器：通过关注犹豫的动态安全监控扩散大语言模型
尽管扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）作为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的替代品已出现，但对D-LLMs的安全监控仍然基本未被探索。与AR-LLMs不同，D-LLMs通过多步骤去噪过程生成文本，暴露出可能包含安全相关信息的中间隐藏表示，而这些信息在标准单步监控设置中不可用。基于轻量级探针适合于始终在线监控的动机，我们分析了哪些轨迹级信号最能指示这些探针可能遇到困难。我们发现，最具信息量的信号是安全犹豫：中间隐藏状态反复落在探针决策边界的小范围内。D-LLM轨迹中这种犹豫步骤的数量有效预测探针失败，提供了样本难度的代理。基于此分析，我们提出了$D^2$-监控器，这是一个针对D-LLMs的双层安全监控器。$D^2$-监控器采用轻量级探针作为始终在线监控器，联合估计犹豫并进行基础分类。当犹豫水平超过阈值时，将激活一个更具表现力但计算负担更重的探针。该动态路由机制在测试时有效分配监控资源。在3个数据集（WildguardMix、ToxicChat、OpenAI-Moderation）上评估4个D-LLMs，$D^2$-监控器以紧凑的参数占用（≤ 0.85M参数）实现了最先进的性能，并在相对于8个基线之间展现了最佳的有效性与效率的权衡。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the gap in safety monitoring for diffusion large language models (D-LLMs), which have not been thoroughly explored compared to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs). Previous methods have primarily focused on single-step monitoring, which fails to utilize the intermediate hidden representations available in D-LLMs that could indicate safety issues. The proposed $D^2$-Monitor introduces a bi-level safety monitoring approach that leverages lightweight probes to continuously assess hesitation signals in the model's trajectory, activating a more complex probe only when necessary. This method effectively predicts probe failure based on the frequency of hesitation steps, allowing for efficient resource allocation during monitoring. Reflect-Guard: Enhancing LLM Safeguards against Adversarial Prompts via Logical Self-Reflection
Authors: Lixing Lin, Juli You, Yue Li, Luyun Lin, Yiqing Wang, Zhen Zhang, Moxuan Zheng
First: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 2 figures, and 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) safety classifiers such as Llama Guard are effective at detecting overtly harmful prompts but remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that disguise malicious intent through role-play scenarios, fictional framing, and indirect requests. We present Reflect-Guard, a method that augments LLM-based safety classifiers with chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Our approach distills analytical reasoning from GPT-4o-mini into structured reflection annotations, then trains Llama-Guard-3-8B via QLoRA to generate logical self-reflections before issuing safety verdicts. Using only 1000 training examples and updating just 0.5% of model parameters (~42M), Reflect-Guard achieves substantial improvements on two challenging benchmarks. On WildGuardTest, F1 score improves from 0.770 to 0.842 (+7.2 pp), with recall on adversarial prompts increasing from 0.513 to 0.921 (+40.8 pp). On JailbreakBench, the attack success rate drops from 10.3% to 1.8%, representing an 82.5% relative reduction. These gains are especially pronounced on adversarial inputs, where the explicit reasoning step enables the model to see through obfuscation techniques that defeat standard pattern-matching approaches. Our results demonstrate that teaching safety classifiers to reason about adversarial intent, rather than simply classify surface patterns, is a promising direction for robust LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Reflect-Guard：通过逻辑自我反思增强大型语言模型对抗性提示的安全防护
大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器如Llama Guard在检测明显有害提示方面有效，但仍然容易受到通过角色扮演场景、虚构框架和间接请求伪装恶意意图的对抗性越狱攻击的影响。我们提出了Reflect-Guard，这是一种通过参数高效微调增强LLM基础安全分类器的链式思维自我反思能力的方法。我们的方法从GPT-4o-mini中提炼分析推理，形成结构化反思注释，然后通过QLoRA训练Llama-Guard-3-8B，以在发出安全裁决之前生成逻辑自我反思。仅使用1000个训练样本，并更新仅0.5%的模型参数（约4200万），Reflect-Guard在两个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了显著改善。在WildGuardTest中，F1分数从0.770提高到0.842（+7.2个百分点），对抗性提示的召回率从0.513提高到0.921（+40.8个百分点）。在JailbreakBench中，攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%，相对减少82.5%。这些提升在对抗性输入上尤为明显，明确的推理步骤使模型能够看穿击败标准模式匹配方法的混淆技术。我们的结果表明，教导安全分类器推理对抗性意图，而不仅仅是分类表面模式，是增强LLM安全性的一个有前景的方向。

The research addresses the limitations of existing large language model (LLM) safety classifiers, which effectively detect harmful prompts but are susceptible to adversarial jailbreak attacks that obscure malicious intent. The proposed Reflect-Guard enhances LLM safety classifiers by integrating chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning, allowing the model to reason about adversarial intent.
